<script type="text/javascript">
    var isMobile = 'False'.toLowerCase() == 'true';

    if (isMobile) {        
        document.getElementById("sub-container-title").addEventListener("click", () => {
            document.getElementById("first-container").style.animation = "mainBack 0.3s forwards";
            document.getElementById("sub-container").style.animation = "subPush 0.3s forwards";
        });

        document.getElementById("second-container-title").addEventListener("click", () => {
            document.getElementById("sub-container").style.animation = "mainBack 0.3s forwards";
            document.getElementById("second-container").style.animation = "subPush 0.3s forwards";
        });
    }

    function goSubContainer(titleChildId, childId) {
        let subCategoryTitleContainer = document.getElementById("sub-container-title");
        let subCategoryContainer = document.getElementById("sub-container-content");
        let categoryChildTitleContainer = document.getElementById(titleChildId);
        let categoryChildContainer = document.getElementById(childId);

        // copy content from childcontainer to sub category content
        subCategoryTitleContainer.innerHTML = categoryChildTitleContainer.innerHTML;
        subCategoryContainer.innerHTML = categoryChildContainer.innerHTML;

        if (isMobile) {
            document.getElementById("first-container").style.animation = "mainAway 0.3s forwards";
            document.getElementById("sub-container").style.animation = "subBack 0.3s forwards";
        } else {
            document.getElementById("sub-container").style.display = "flex";
        }
    }

    function goChildContainer(titleChildrenId, ChildrenId) {
        let subCategoryChildrenTitleContainer = document.getElementById("second-container-title");
        let subCategoryChildrenContainer = document.getElementById("second-container-content");
        let categoryChildrenTitleContainer = document.getElementById(titleChildrenId);

        let categoryChildContainer = document.getElementById(ChildrenId);
        // copy content from childcontainer to sub category content
        subCategoryChildrenTitleContainer.innerHTML = categoryChildrenTitleContainer.innerHTML;
        subCategoryChildrenContainer.innerHTML = categoryChildContainer.innerHTML;

        document.getElementById("sub-container").style.animation = "mainAway 0.3s forwards";
        document.getElementById("second-container").style.animation = "subBack 0.3s forwards";
    }
    </script>

<script>
    var ValueSearchStore = null;
    function changeOnOff(e) {
        var elements = document.getElementsByClassName("searchStoreClass");
        if (elements.length > 0) {
            if (elements[0].value == "on") {
                ValueSearchStore = "off";
                for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
                    elements[i].value = "off";
                }
            }
            else {
                ValueSearchStore = "on";
                for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
                    elements[i].value = "on";
                }
            }
        }
    }
</script>

<script>
    var viewport = document.querySelector("meta[name=viewport]");
    var storeSearch = document.getElementById("search-store");
    var navbarHeight = document.getElementById("navbar").clientHeight;
    var countDown = document.getElementById("countdown");
    document.getElementById("inputSearchV2").onfocus = function () {
        storeSearch.style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById("main-container").style.paddingTop = navbarHeight + 30 + 'px';
        document.getElementById("main-container").style.marginTop = '0px';
        if (countDown != null) {
            countDown.style.marginTop = '34px';
        }
        viewport.setAttribute('content', 'width=device-width,  initial-scale=1.0, user-scalable=0');
    };
    function rollback() {
        viewport.setAttribute('content', ' initial-scale=1.0, user-scalable=1');
    }
</script>

<script>
    var ValueSearchStore = null;
    function changeOnOff(e) {
        var elements = document.getElementsByClassName("searchStoreClass");
        if (elements.length > 0) {
            if (elements[0].value == "on") {
                ValueSearchStore = "off";
                for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
                    elements[i].value = "off";
                }
            }
            else {
                ValueSearchStore = "on";
                for (var i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
                    elements[i].value = "on";
                }
            }
        }
    }
</script>
<script type="text/javascript">

            var homeUrl = "https://juntoz.com/";
            var scheme = "https://";
        </script>
<script>
    var viewport = document.querySelector("meta[name=viewport]");
    var storeSearch = document.getElementById("search-store");
    var navbarHeight = document.getElementById("navbar").clientHeight;
    var countDown = document.getElementById("countdown");
    document.getElementById("inputSearchV2").onfocus = function () {
        storeSearch.style.display = 'block';
        document.getElementById("main-container").style.paddingTop = navbarHeight + 30 + 'px';
        document.getElementById("main-container").style.marginTop = '0px';
        if (countDown != null) {
            countDown.style.marginTop = '34px';
        }
        viewport.setAttribute('content', 'width=device-width,  initial-scale=1.0, user-scalable=0');
    };
    function rollback() {
        viewport.setAttribute('content', ' initial-scale=1.0, user-scalable=1');
    }
</script>

<script type="text/javascript">
    var userId = '';
    var userEmail = '';
    var isMobile = 'False'.toLowerCase() == 'true';
    var sideMenuIcon = document.getElementById("hm-icon-container");

    // TODO: header menu should be a component
    var insideCoverHamburguerElement = document.getElementById("hm-button");
    insideCoverHamburguerElement.addEventListener("click", sideBarEvent);

    function sideBarEvent() {
        if (sideMenuIcon.classList.contains("hm-show-icon")) {
            showSideBarRightEvent();
        } else {
            hideSideBarRightEvent();
        }
    }

    function showSideBarRightEvent() {
        let bodyNodeHTML = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];
        let backgroundOverLay = document.getElementById("overlay");
        let closeBtn = document.getElementById("close-btn");

        document.getElementById("juntoz-sidenav").style.animation = "expand 0.3s forwards";
        document.getElementById("juntoz-sidenav").style.display = "block";
        // Overlay
        backgroundOverLay.style.display = "block";
        backgroundOverLay.style.animation = "show 0.3s";
        // closeBtn
        closeBtn.style.display = "block";
        closeBtn.style.animation = "show 0.3s";

        bodyNodeHTML.style.overflowY = "hidden";

        //sideMenuIcon.classList.remove("hm-show-icon");
        //sideMenuIcon.classList.add("hm-close-icon");
    }

    function hideSideBarRightEvent() {
        let bodyNodeHTML = document.getElementsByTagName("body")[0];

        document.getElementById("juntoz-sidenav").style.animation = "collapse 0.3s forwards";
        document.getElementById("overlay").style.animation = "hide 0.3s";
        document.getElementById("close-btn").style.animation = "hide 0.3s";

        if (!isMobile) {
            document.getElementById('sub-container').style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("juntoz-sidenav").style.animation = "collapse 0.3s forwards";
        }

        bodyNodeHTML.style.overflowY = "auto";

        setTimeout(() => {
            document.getElementById("overlay").style.display = "none";
            document.getElementById("close-btn").style.display = "none";
            // Reset Menus
            if (isMobile) {
                document.getElementById("first-container").style.animation = "";
                document.getElementById("first-container").style.transform = "translateX(0px)";
                document.getElementById("sub-container").style.animation = "";
                document.getElementById("sub-container").style.transform = "translateX(380px)";
                document.getElementById("second-container").style.animation = "";
                document.getElementById("second-container").style.transform = "translateX(380px)";
            }
        }, 300);
    }
</script>

<script>
    function searchBrand() {
    var input, filter, ul, li, span, i, txtValue;
    input = document.getElementById("inputSearchBrand");
    filter = input.value.toUpperCase();
    ul = document.getElementById("listOfBrands");
    li = ul.getElementsByTagName("li");
    for (i = 0; i < li.length; i++) {
        span = li[i].getElementsByTagName("span")[0];
        txtValue = span.textContent || span.innerText;
        if (txtValue.toUpperCase().indexOf(filter) > -1) {
            li[i].style.display = "";
        } else {
            li[i].style.display = "none";
        }
    }
}
</script>
</div>

<script>
    var sumar = document.getElementById("modal-shopping-add");
    var restar = document.getElementById("modal-shopping-sub");
    var contador = document.getElementById("modal-shopping-quantity");

    function calcular(value) {
        let isValid = /^[0-9][0-9]*$/.test(value);
        if (isValid) {
            let minQuantity = 1;
            let maxQuantity = $("#modal-shopping-cart").data("maxQuantity");
            let modalAlert = $("#modal-alert");

            if (maxQuantity > 0 && value > maxQuantity) {
                sumar.disabled = true;
                modalAlert.show();
            }
            else if (value < minQuantity) {
                restar.disabled = true;
            }
            else {
                contador.value = value;
                sumar.disabled = false;
                restar.disabled = false;
                modalAlert.hide();
                updateCart(value);
            }            
        }
    }

    sumar.onclick = function () {
        value = Number(contador.value) + 1;
        calcular(value);
    };

    restar.onclick = function () {
        value = Number(contador.value) - 1;
        calcular(value);
    };

    function xhrCart(url, data) {
        return $.ajax({
            url: url,
            type: 'POST',
            data: JSON.stringify(data),
            processData: false,
            cache: false,
            contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
            datatype: 'json',
        });
    };

    function updateCart(value) {
        $('#cart__items__preloader').show();

        var seoUrl = $("#modal-shopping-cart").data("id");

        xhrCart('/cart/update/' + seoUrl + '/' + parseInt(value)).done(function (response) {
            if (!response.isSuccess) {
                let errors = [];
                sessionStorage.setItem("hasErrors", "true");
                errors.push(response.message);
                sessionStorage.setItem("errors", JSON.stringify(errors));
            }

            //Get Items Cart
            $.getJSON("/cart/summary", function (data) {
                var total = data.totalItems;
                $('.icon-cart__badge').text(total);
            });

            $('#cart__items__preloader').hide();
        });
    }

    /* for add to Cart from Catalog Components */
    function productClick(id) {
        var products = jzTagManager.qs.getObjectScope("productInfo")
        var item = products.filter(function (i) {
            return i.productStoreId == id;
        })
        jzTagManager.productClick(item[0])
    }

    async function addToCartFromCatalog(event, product) {
        
        let { id, productStoreId, name, image, symbol, specialPrice, price, hasSpecialPrice, maxQuantity} = product;
        jzTagManager.addToCart();

        let previousValue = event.target.innerHTML;
        event.preventDefault();
        event.target.disabled = true;
        event.target.innerHTML = "<i class='fa fa-refresh fa-spin fa-lg fa-fw'>";

        try {
            var affiliateCode = localStorage.getItem('code');
            let construct = {
                url: '/cart/add',
                data: JSON.stringify({
                    id: id,
                    productStoreId: productStoreId,
                    associatedOffer: product.associatedOffer,
                    Qty: 1,
                    code: affiliateCode
                })
            };

            let request = await $.ajax({
                url: construct.url,
                type: 'POST',
                data: construct.data,
                processData: false,
                cache: false,
                contentType: "application/json; charset=utf-8",
                datatype: 'json'
            });

            //Get Items Cart
            let { cartItems, totalItems } = await $.getJSON("/cart/summary");
            let item = cartItems.find(el => el.productStoreId == productStoreId);
            let quantity = item != null ? item.quantity : 1;
            
            $("#modal-shopping-cart").data("id", id);
            $("#modal-shopping-cart").data("maxQuantity", maxQuantity);
            $("#modal-shopping-name").text(name);
            $("#modal-shopping-image").attr("src", image);
            $("#modal-shopping-sprice").text(symbol + specialPrice);
            $("#modal-shopping-price").text(symbol + price);
            if (!hasSpecialPrice) $("#modal-shopping-price").hide();
            $("#modal-shopping-quantity").val(quantity);
            $("#modal-shopping-cart").modal();

            $('.icon-cart__badge').text(totalItems);

        } catch (err) {

            let reason = err.responseJSON;

            if (reason && reason.isSuccess !== "undefined" && reason.isSuccess === false) {
                toastr.warning(reason.message);
            }
            else {
                toastr.error('Hubo un problema, vuelve a intentar por favor.');
            }
        }

        event.target.disabled = false;
        event.target.innerHTML = previousValue;
    }
</script>
